  <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
   // Javascript to sort out the highlighting of the top navigation since we can't give the body an ID in the CMS
        $(window).load(function () {

            // initialise plugins
            jQuery(function () {

                jQuery('ul.sf-menu').supersubs({
                    minWidth: 15,   // minimum width of sub-menus in em units 
                    maxWidth: 27,   // maximum width of sub-menus in em units 
                    extraWidth: 1     // extra width can ensure lines don't sometimes turn over 
                    // due to slight rounding differences and font-family 
                }).superfish({
                    autoArrows: false
                });
            });

            // Get the current url
            var currlocation = window.location.pathname;

            var regExHome = new RegExp("magazine.aspx");
            var regExAlt = new RegExp("/magazine/");
            if (regExHome.test(currlocation) || regExAlt.test(currlocation)) {
                $('#nav-magazine').addClass('current');
                return;
            }
            regExHome = new RegExp("celebs.aspx");
            regExAlt = new RegExp("/celebs/");
            if (regExHome.test(currlocation) || regExAlt.test(currlocation)) {
                $('#nav-celebs').addClass('current');
                return;
            }
            regExHome = new RegExp("guides.aspx");
            regExAlt = new RegExp("/guides/");
            if (regExHome.test(currlocation) || regExAlt.test(currlocation)) {
                $('#nav-guides').addClass('current');
                return;
            }
            regExHome = new RegExp("exhibition.aspx");
            regExAlt = new RegExp("/exhibition/");
            if (regExHome.test(currlocation) || regExAlt.test(currlocation)) {
                $('#nav-exhibition').addClass('current');
                return;
            }
            regExHome = new RegExp("news.aspx");
            regExAlt = new RegExp("/news/");
            if (regExHome.test(currlocation) || regExAlt.test(currlocation)) {
                $('#nav-news').addClass('current');
                return;
            }
            regExHome = new RegExp("tvshow.aspx");
            regExAlt = new RegExp("/tvshow/");
            if (regExHome.test(currlocation) || regExAlt.test(currlocation)) {
                $('#nav-tv').addClass('current');
                return;
            }
            regExHome = new RegExp("sellyourproperty.aspx");
            regExAlt = new RegExp("/sellyourproperty/");
            if (regExHome.test(currlocation) || regExAlt.test(currlocation)) {
                $('#nav-sell').addClass('current');
                return;
            }

            $('#nav-home').addClass('current');

        });
  </script>

    //&lt;![CDATA[
document.forms['aspnetForm'].action='/AP1593959/Infinite-Pool-next-to-Obidos/';var myForm = document.forms['aspnetForm'];
if (!myForm) {
   myForm = document.aspnetForm;
}
function doCustomPostBack(commandName, commandArgument, doConfirm, message) {
   if (!myForm.onsubmit || (myForm.onsubmit() != false)) {
       if (doConfirm == true) {
           var agree = confirm(message);
           if (agree == true) {
               doCustomSubmit(commandName, commandArgument);
           }
       } else {
           doCustomSubmit(commandName, commandArgument);
       }
   }
}
function doCustomSubmit(commandName, commandArgument) {
   myForm.CUSTOMCOMMANDNAME.value = commandName;
   myForm.CUSTOMCOMMANDARGUMENT.value = commandArgument;
   myForm.submit();
}
//]]&gt;

   <script type="text/javascript">
    //&lt;![CDATA[

var gListingReference;
function shortlist(listingReference) {
   gListingReference=listingReference;
   var button=document.getElementById('shortlist_'+listingReference);
   button.disabled=true;
   button.value='Updating...';
$.ajax({
type: "POST",
url: "/ws/Shortlist.asmx/AddToShortlist",
data: "listingReference=" + listingReference , 
error: function (XMLHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrown) {
alert(errorThrown);
} , 
success: function(data, textStatus) {
    var result;$(data).find('string').each(function() { 
 result = $(this).text();
 })
   button.disabled=false;
   switch (result) {
       case "Shortlisted":
           button.value='Saved';
           $("#shortlist_"+listingReference).removeClass('addOption_button');$("#shortlist_"+listingReference).addClass('addOption_button_disabled');
           changeShortlistCounterText(1);
           break;
       case "NotShortlisted":
           button.value='Add to shortlist';
           $("#shortlist_"+listingReference).removeClass('addOption_button_disabled');$("#shortlist_"+listingReference).addClass('addOption_button');
           changeShortlistCounterText(-1);
           break;
       case "LimitReached":
           button.value='Add to shortlist';
           alert('Sorry, you have reached your Favourites limit.\n\nYou can save up to 50 items in your Favourites.\nTo add any more please delete some items first.');
           break;
       default:
           button.value='error';
           button.style.background="transparent url('/images/ukdestinations/buying/forms/button_wide_disabled.gif') no-repeat";
           alert('Sorry, an error occurred with your Favourites.\n\nPlease try again.');
           break;

   }
}
});
}
function shortlistMouseover(button) {
   if (button.value=='Saved') {
       button.value='Remove';
   }
}
function shortlistMouseout(button) {
   if (button.value=='Remove') {
       button.value='Saved';
   }
}
function changeShortlistCounterText(amount){
   var counter=document.getElementById('shortlistCount');
   if(counter!=null){
      document.getElementById('shortlistCount').innerHTML=parseInt(document.getElementById('shortlistCount').innerHTML)+amount;
   }
}
//]]&gt;
   </script>

       $(document).ready(function () {
        $('.ui-widget-overlay').live('click', function () {            
            $("#popupMailForm").dialog("close");
            $('#' + 'ctl00_Main_ListingShareOptionsControl_txtName' + '_InternalTextBox').empty();
            $('#' + 'ctl00_Main_ListingShareOptionsControl_txtEmailAddress' + '_InternalTextBox').empty();
            $('#' + 'ctl00_Main_ListingShareOptionsControl_txtFriendsEmailAddresses' + '_InternalTextBox').val('');
            $('#' + 'ctl00_Main_ListingShareOptionsControl_txtComments' + '_InternalTextBox').val('');
            $('#' + 'ctl00_Main_ListingShareOptionsControl_lbEmailAdressError').empty();
            $('#' + 'ctl00_Main_ListingShareOptionsControl_lbFriendsEmailAddresses').empty();
        });     
    });

    function ShowPopupMailForm() {
        $("#popupMailForm").dialog({
            modal: true,
            width: 480,
            height: 450,
            left: 720,
            dialogClass: "popupMailForm-no-close",
            appendTo: $("form:first"),
            open: function (event, ui) {
                $(".ui-widget-overlay").css({
                    opacity: 0.5,
                    filter: "Alpha(Opacity=50)",
                    background: "black"
                });
            },
            close: function (event, ui) {
                $('#' + 'ctl00_Main_ListingShareOptionsControl_txtName' + '_InternalTextBox').empty();
                $('#' + 'ctl00_Main_ListingShareOptionsControl_txtEmailAddress' + '_InternalTextBox').val('');
                $('#' + 'ctl00_Main_ListingShareOptionsControl_txtFriendsEmailAddresses' + '_InternalTextBox').val('');
                $('#' + 'ctl00_Main_ListingShareOptionsControl_txtComments' + '_InternalTextBox').val('');
                $('#' + 'ctl00_Main_ListingShareOptionsControl_lbEmailAdressError').empty();
                $('#' + 'ctl00_Main_ListingShareOptionsControl_lbFriendsEmailAddresses').empty();
            },
            resizable: false
        });

        $('.ui-dialog').css('z-index', 1130);
        $('.ui-widget-overlay').css('z-index', 1102);
        $(".ui-widget").css({ height: "0px" });
        $(".ui-widget").css({ width: "0px" });
        $(".ui-widget-overlay").appendTo($("form:first"));
        $(".ui-widget textarea").css({ "font-size": "11px" });
    }

    function ShowSuccess() {
        $("#popupMailFormSuccess").dialog({
            modal: true,
            width: 480,
            height: 135,
            left: 720,
            dialogClass: "popupMailForm-no-close",
            appendTo: $("form:first"),
            open: function (event, ui) {
                $(".ui-widget-overlay").css({
                    opacity: 0.5,
                    filter: "Alpha(Opacity=50)",
                    background: "black"
                });
            },
            resizable: false
        });
        $('.ui-dialog').css('z-index', 1130);
        $('.ui-widget-overlay').css('z-index', 1102);
        $(".ui-widget").css({ height: "0px" });
        $(".ui-widget").css({ width: "0px" });
        $(".ui-widget-content").css({ border: "0px" });
        $(".ui-widget").css({ background: "transparent" });
        $(".ui-widget-overlay").appendTo($("form:first"));
    }
    function CloseSuccessMailForm() {
        $("#popupMailFormSuccess").find("form").remove();
        $("#popupMailFormSuccess").dialog('destroy');
    }

    function forcebtnSendClick() {
        __doPostBack('ctl00$Main$ListingShareOptionsControl$SendButton','');
    }
